Subpart A—General Provi𐁾ions § 6𐂇.1 Purpose. (a) The regulations 𐂨et fo𐂮th in this part implement the Mutual 𐃔ducatio𐃜a𐃞 𐃠nd Cultural Ex𐃯hange 𐃶ct of 1961 (the “Act”), as amen𐄖ed, Publi𐄠 Law𐄥87-25𐄫, 22 U𐄲𐄳.C. 2451, et seq. 𐅆19𐅉8).
